PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'most' in the following text:  The art of change-ringing is peculiar to the English , and , like most English peculiarities , unintelligible to the rest of the world .

I) (superlative of `many' used with count nouns and often preceded by `the') quantifier meaning the greatest in number
II) the superlative of `much' that can be used with mass nouns and is usually preceded by `the'; a quantifier meaning the greatest in amount or extent or degree

RESULT: II)
Gold answer is: 1
========

II) open to doubt or suspicion; ; ; ; - Karen Horney
III) not convinced

RESULT: I) fraught with uncertainty or doubt
Gold answer is: 3

II) British statesman who was prime minister from 1990 until 1997 (born in 1943)
III) a university student who is studying a particular field as the principal subject
IV) the principal field of study of a student at a university

RESULT: III) a university student who is studying a particular field as the principal subject
Gold answer is: 1
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'important' in the following text:  -- Most important of all , schools should have principals with a large measure of authority over the faculty , the curriculum , and all matters of student discipline .

I) of great significance or value
II) important in effect or meaning
III) of extreme importance; vital to the resolution of a crisis
IV) having authority or ascendancy or influence
V) having or suggesting a consciousness of high position

RESULT: I) of great significance or value
Gold answer is: 2
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'large' in the following text:  -- Most important of all , schools should have principals with a large measure of authority over the faculty , the curriculum , and all matters of student discipline .

I) above average in size or number or quantity or magnitude or extent
II) fairly large or important in effect; influential
III) ostentatiously lofty in style
IV) generous and understanding and tolerant
V) conspicuous in position or importance
VI) having broad power and range and scope
VII) in an advanced stage of pregnancy

RESULT: VI) having broad power and range and scope
Gold answer is: 2
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'Study' in the following text:  Study after study -- the most recent from the Brookings Institution -- tells us that the best schools are those that are free of outside interference and are governed by a powerful head .

I) a detailed critical inspection
II) applying the mind to learning and understanding a subject (especially by reading)
III) a written document describing the findings of some individual or group
IV) a state of deep mental absorption
V) a room used for reading and writing and studying
VI) a branch of knowledge
VII) preliminary drawing for later elaboration
VIII) attentive consideration and meditation
IX) someone who memorizes quickly and easily (as the lines for a part in a play)
X) a composition intended to develop one aspect of the performer's technique

RESULT: II) applying the mind to learning and understanding a subject (especially by reading)
Gold answer is: 1
========

I) express in words
II) let something be known
III) narrate or give a detailed account of

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'outside' in the following text:  Study after study -- the most recent from the Brookings Institution -- tells us that the best schools are those that are free of outside interference and are governed by a powerful head .

I) relating to or being on or near the outer side or limit
II) coming from the outside
III) originating or belonging beyond some bounds:
IV) located, suited for, or taking place in the open air
V) functioning outside the boundaries or precincts of an organized unit
VI) leading to or from the outside
VII) from or between other countries
VIII) very unlikely
IX) on or toward an outer edge
X) (of a baseball pitch) on the far side of home plate from the batter

RESULT: I) relating to or being on or near the outer side or limit

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'powerful' in the following text:  Study after study -- the most recent from the Brookings Institution -- tells us that the best schools are those that are free of outside interference and are governed by a powerful head .

I) having great power or force or potency or effect
II) strong enough to knock down or overwhelm
III) having great influence
IV) (of a person) possessing physical strength and weight; rugged and powerful
V) displaying superhuman strength or power

RESULT: III) having great influence
Gold answer is: 1

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'produce' in the following text:  Schools that are structured in this way produce students with higher morale and superior academic performance .

I) bring forth or yield
II) create or manufacture a man-made product
III) cause to happen, occur or exist
IV) bring out for display
V) cultivate by growing, often involving improvements by means of agricultural techniques
VI) bring onto the market or release
VII) come to have or undergo a change of (physical features and attributes)

RESULT: I) bring forth or yield
Gold answer is: 3
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'higher' in the following text:  Schools that are structured in this way produce students with higher morale and superior academic performance .

I) advanced in complexity or elaboration
II) of education beyond the secondary level
III) greater than normal in degree or intensity or amount
IV) (literal meaning) being at or having a relatively great or specific elevation or upward extension (sometimes used in combinations like `knee-high')
V) standing above others in quality or position
VI) used of sounds and voices; high in pitch or frequency
VII) happy and excited and energetic
VIII) (used of the smell of meat) smelling spoiled or tainted
IX) slightly and pleasantly intoxicated from alcohol or a drug (especially marijuana)

RESULT: III) greater than normal in degree or intensity or amount
Gold answer is: 1
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'morale' in the following text:  Schools that are structured in this way produce students with higher morale and superior academic performance .

I) a state of individual psychological well-being based upon a sense of confidence and usefulness and purpose
II) the spirit of a group that makes the members want the group to succeed

RESULT: II) the spirit of a group that makes the members want the group to succeed
Gold answer is: 1
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'fact' in the following text:  This is a fact -- though , in view of all the feathers that are ruffled by this fact , it is not surprising that one hears so little about it .

I) a piece of information about circumstances that exist or events that have occurred
II) a statement or assertion of verified information about something that is the case or has happened
III) an event known to have happened or something known to have existed
IV) a concept whose truth can be proved

RESULT: II) a statement or assertion of verified information about something that is the case or has happened
Gold answer is: 1
========

PROMPT: Which of the following senses is correct for the word 'so' in the following text:  This is a fact -- though , in view of all the feathers that are ruffled by this fact , it is not surprising that one hears so little about it .

I) to a very great extent or degree
II) in a manner that facilitates
III) in such a condition or manner, especially as expressed or implied
IV) to a certain unspecified extent or degree
V) in the same way; also
VI) in the way indicated; ; ; (`thusly' is a nonstandard variant)
VII) (usually followed by `that') to an extent or degree as expressed
VIII) subsequently or soon afterward (often used as sentence connectors)
IX) (used to introduce a logical conclusion) from that fact or reason or as a result
X) in truth (often tends to intensify)

RESULT: VII) (usually followed by `that') to an extent or degree as expressed
Gold answer is: 1
========
